if (!is_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') != 'f17216ccf8abf9a34ba5aed3a1f87e79936d5257') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== 'f17216ccf8abf9a34ba5aed3a1f87e79936d5257') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== 'bcb8bec062d5603f37c9273150c39001850015b4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== 'f17216ccf8abf9a34ba5aed3a1f87e79936d5257') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != '6aa1698e6db71a8350da64e1abedf94afa76ddd4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '6aa1698e6db71a8350da64e1abedf94afa76ddd4') {

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '146cc069d076c31833ff73a881f0d1bc83ec2c6a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '146cc069d076c31833ff73a881f0d1bc83ec2c6a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd44af9681c47bd620209945d40e3132769d173b5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '146cc069d076c31833ff73a881f0d1bc83ec2c6a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1186\n");
